We contend that a feed-forward paradigm, leveraging multi-frame context to predict Gaussian attributes directly, is crucial for addressing these challenges. We present Flash-Mono, a system composed of three core modules: a feed-forward prediction frontend, a 2D Gaussian Splatting mapping backend, and an efficient hidden-state-based loop closure module. We trained a recurrent feed-forward frontend model that progressively aggregates multi-frame visual features into a hidden state via cross attention and jointly predicts camera poses and per-pixel Gaussian properties. By directly predicting Gaussian attributes, our method bypasses the burdensome per-frame optimization required in optimization-based GS-SLAM, achieving a $\textbf{10x}$ speedup while ensuring high-quality rendering. The power of our recurrent architecture extends beyond efficient prediction. The hidden states act as compact submap descriptors, facilitating efficient loop closure and global $\mathrm{Sim}(3)$ optimization to mitigate the long-standing challenge of drift. For enhanced geometric fidelity, we replace conventional 3D Gaussian ellipsoids with 2D Gaussian surfels. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Flash-Mono achieves state-of-the-art performance in both tracking and mapping quality, highlighting its potential for embodied perception and real-time reconstruction applications. Project page: https://victkk.github.io/flash-mono.

We present an open-source off-road navigation stack supporting both LiDAR and monocular 3D perception without task-specific training. For the monocular setup, we combine zero-shot depth prediction (Depth Anything V2) with metric depth rescaling using sparse SLAM measurements (VINS-Mono). The resulting point cloud is used to generate a robot-centric 2.5D elevation map for costmap-based planning. *Mingao Tan,Yiyang Li,Shanze Wang,Xinming Zhang,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出FSUNav系统，一种结合大脑—小脑结构的视觉-语言导航方法，实现了多机器人、零样本、开放词汇和多模态输入条件下的高效、安全导航。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言导航方法在支持不同类型机器人、实时性和安全性方面受限，且难以泛化到新语义和多模态任务输入，妨碍了其实际部署和广泛应用。

Method: FSUNav采纳大脑-小脑结构：小脑模块通过深度强化学习实现通用的本地路径规划，适配多种机器人并减少碰撞风险；大脑模块利用视觉-语言模型，搭建三层推理体系，实现开放词汇、零样本的目标检测和验证。整体框架支持文本、描述、图像等多模态输入。

Result: 在MP3D、HM3D及OVON基准上，FSUNav在目标导航、实例图像和任务导航任务表现出SOTA水平，显著优于现有方法。多种机器人平台的实际部署也验证了其强健性和实用价值。

Conclusion: FSUNav突破了传统视觉-语言导航方法的局限，实现了异构机器人间的高效泛化、安全鲁棒的零样本导航，对实际智能机器人广泛应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Current vision-language navigation methods face substantial bottlenecks regarding heterogeneous robot compatibility, real-time performance, and navigation safety. Furthermore, they struggle to support open-vocabulary semantic generalization and multimodal task inputs. To address these challenges, this paper proposes FSUNav: a Cerebrum-Cerebellum architecture for fast, safe, and universal zero-shot goal-oriented navigation, which innovatively integrates vision-language models (VLMs) with the proposed architecture. The cerebellum module, a high-frequency end-to-end module, develops a universal local planner based on deep reinforcement learning, enabling unified navigation across heterogeneous platforms (e.g., humanoid, quadruped, wheeled robots) to improve navigation efficiency while significantly reducing collision risk. The cerebrum module constructs a three-layer reasoning model and leverages VLMs to build an end-to-end detection and verification mechanism, enabling zero-shot open-vocabulary goal navigation without predefined IDs and improving task success rates in both simulation and real-world environments. Additionally, the framework supports multimodal inputs (e.g., text, target descriptions, and images), further enhancing generalization, real-time performance, safety, and robustness. Experimental results on MP3D, HM3D, and OVON benchmarks demonstrate that FSUNav achieves state-of-the-art performance on object, instance image, and task navigation, significantly outperforming existing methods. Real-world deployments on diverse robotic platforms further validate its robustness and practical applicability.

</details>


### [189] [Multi-View Video Diffusion Policy: A 3D Spatio-Temporal-Aware Video Action Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03181)
*Peiyan Li,Yixiang Chen,Yuan Xu,Jiabing Yang,Xiangnan Wu,Jun Guo,Nan Sun,Long Qian,Xinghang Li,Xin Xiao,Jing Liu,Nianfeng Liu,Tao Kong,Yan Huang,Liang Wang,Tieniu Tan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: MV-VDP是一种多视角视频扩散策略，可联合建模环境的3D时空状态，显著提升了机器人操作的效率与泛化能力，尤其在数据有限时表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的机器人操作策略多依赖于2D视觉观测和基于静态图片-文本对的预训练模型，对环境动态理解有限，导致对数据依赖大且泛化能力弱。该工作旨在解决现有方法对环境状态和动态建模的不足。

Method: 提出MV-VDP（多视角视频扩散策略），通过同时预测多视角热力图视频和RGB视频，将视频预训练与动作微调的表示对齐，并能明确编码环境对机器人动作的预期响应。通过这样联合的3D时空建模，强化了对动作和环境动态的理解。

Result: MV-VDP仅通过10条示范轨迹、无须额外预训练，即可在复杂现实任务上取得高效的操作表现，对模型超参数较为鲁棒，能泛化到分布外环境并预测真实未来场景。多个实验表明MV-VDP在数据效率、多任务操作等方面优于基于视频预测、3D建模和视觉-语言-动作的主流模型。

Conclusion: MV-VDP不仅极大减少了机器人操作对数据的需求，提升了鲁棒性和可解释性，还在多任务、多场景下实现了新的性能标杆，为3D时空感知驱动的机器人操作开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Robotic manipulation requires understanding both the 3D spatial structure of the environment and its temporal evolution, yet most existing policies overlook one or both. They typically rely on 2D visual observations and backbones pretrained on static image--text pairs, resulting in high data requirements and limited understanding of environment dynamics. To address this, we introduce MV-VDP, a multi-view video diffusion policy that jointly models the 3D spatio-temporal state of the environment. The core idea is to simultaneously predict multi-view heatmap videos and RGB videos, which 1) align the representation format of video pretraining with action finetuning, and 2) specify not only what actions the robot should take, but also how the environment is expected to evolve in response to those actions. Extensive experiments show that MV-VDP enables data-efficient, robust, generalizable, and interpretable manipulation. With only ten demonstration trajectories and without additional pretraining, MV-VDP successfully performs complex real-world tasks, demonstrates strong robustness across a range of model hyperparameters, generalizes to out-of-distribution settings, and predicts realistic future videos. Experiments on Meta-World and real-world robotic platforms demonstrate that MV-VDP consistently outperforms video-prediction--based, 3D-based, and vision--language--action models, establishing a new state of the art in data-efficient multi-task manipulation.

</details>


### [190] [The Compression Gap: Why Discrete Tokenization Limits Vision-Language-Action Model Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03191)
*Takuya Shiba*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型中升级视觉编码器是否能提升下游任务表现，发现只在动作为连续表示时有效，而离散化的动作表示存在信息瓶颈，限制了视觉编码器改进的效益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLA模型普遍认为增强视觉编码器能力能带来整体表现提升，但为何这种直觉在不同动作表示下表现不一仍未明确。

Method: 作者在LIBERO基准下，通过多项实验证明：1）在动作为连续表示（如Diffusion Policy）时，升级视觉编码器带来明显增益；2）在动作为固定容量码本离散表示（如OAT）下，即便编码器升级，表现提升有限；3）通过调整码本容量提供因果证据，验证信息瓶颈假设。此外，还测试了不同视觉编码器带来的影响。

Result: 实验展示，Diffusion Policy下视觉编码器升级可带来21个百分点以上提升，而OAT模型表现基本不变。调整码本容量后，OAT对编码器质量的敏感性有所恢复，证实信息瓶颈的位置决定了扩展效益。

Conclusion: 在物理智能（Physical AI）中模型性能扩展受限于系统中的信息瓶颈，必须先找准瓶颈所在，而不是盲目提升模型或数据规模才能取得实际增益。

Abstract: Scaling Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models by upgrading the vision encoder is expected to improve downstream manipulation performance--as it does in vision-language modeling. We show that this expectation fails when actions are represented as discrete tokens, and explain why through an information-theoretic principle we call the Compression Gap: in any visuomotor pipeline, scaling behavior is governed by the location of the tightest information bottleneck. When actions are continuous (e.g., Diffusion Policy), the vision encoder is the binding constraint, and upgrading it directly improves performance. When actions are discretized through a fixed-capacity codebook (e.g., OAT), the codebook becomes the binding constraint, and encoder improvements cannot propagate past it--regardless of how rich the upstream representation is. We validate this principle on the LIBERO benchmark with three lines of evidence: a factorial experiment showing that encoder upgrades improve Diffusion Policy by over 21 percentage points while OAT gains are substantially attenuated across model scales; an encoder quality gradient across four encoders confirming that Diffusion Policy tracks encoder quality monotonically while OAT remains flat; and a codebook size experiment demonstrating that relaxing codebook capacity partially recovers encoder sensitivity, providing causal evidence for the bottleneck hypothesis. Our findings reveal that scaling in Physical AI requires identifying where information bottlenecks lie in the pipeline, rather than uniformly increasing model or data size.

</details>


### [191] [Safety-Critical Centralized Nonlinear MPC for Cooperative Payload Transportation by Two Quadrupedal Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03200)
*Ruturaj S. Sambhus,Yicheng Zeng,Kapi Ketan Mehta,Jeeseop Kim,Kaveh Akbari Hamed*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于两台四足机器人协作搬运物体的安全关键型集中非线性模型预测控制（NMPC）框架，实现了在复杂环境下的安全协作搬运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对多机器人协作搬运任务中，受环境复杂性、物体动力学耦合、碰撞风险及不确定扰动等因素的挑战，亟需一种高效、安全且能够处理复杂约束的控制方法。

Method: 将机器人-物体系统建模为离散时间非线性微分代数系统，通过完整约束与交互力来描述系统耦合。结合控制障碍函数（CBF）与NMPC，建立包含碰撞回避、安全约束、将交互力视为决策变量的最优控制问题，实现实时高效控制。

Result: 算法在两个Unitree Go2机器人平台上进行了大量硬件实验，在杂乱环境、质量和惯量不确定性以及外部推力干扰下，验证了搬运任务的安全性和有效性。

Conclusion: 所提安全关键性集中NMPC方法能够实现多四足机器人在复杂环境下的安全协作搬运，具有良好的实时性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: This paper presents a safety-critical centralized nonlinear model predictive control (NMPC) framework for cooperative payload transportation by two quadrupedal robots. The interconnected robot-payload system is modeled as a discrete-time nonlinear differential-algebraic system, capturing the coupled dynamics through holonomic constraints and interaction wrenches. To ensure safety in complex environments, we develop a control barrier function (CBF)-based NMPC formulation that enforces collision avoidance constraints for both the robots and the payload. The proposed approach retains the interaction wrenches as decision variables, resulting in a structured DAE-constrained optimal control problem that enables efficient real-time implementation. The effectiveness of the algorithm is validated through extensive hardware experiments on two Unitree Go2 platforms performing cooperative payload transportation in cluttered environments under mass and inertia uncertainty and external push disturbances.

</details>
